         <p>
          <b>
           Cradily
          </b>
          (
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Japanese_Pok%C3%A9mon_names" title="List of Japanese Pokmon names">
           Japanese
          </a>
          :
          <b>
           
          </b>
          <i>
           Yuradle
          </i>
          ) is a dual-type
          <a href="/wiki/Rock_(type)" title="Rock (type)">
           Rock
          </a>
          /
          <a href="/wiki/Grass_(type)" title="Grass (type)">
           Grass
          </a>
          <a href="/wiki/Fossil" title="Fossil">
           Fossil
          </a>
          Pokmon.
         </p>
         <p>
          It
          <a href="/wiki/Evolution" title="Evolution">
           evolves
          </a>
          from
          <a href="/wiki/Lileep_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Lileep (Pokmon)">
           Lileep
          </a>
          starting at
          <a href="/wiki/Level" title="Level">
           level
          </a>
          40, after it is revived from a
          <a href="/wiki/Root_and_Claw_Fossils" title="Root and Claw Fossils">
           Root Fossil
          </a>
          .
         </p>

         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Biology">
           Biology
          </span>
         </h2>
         <p>
          Cradily is a green, plant-like Pokmon with various yellow markings on its head, neck, and torso. There are circular, yellow eyespots on its head. However, its true eyes are concealed inside the dark, crescent opening on its head. Surrounding its head at the base are eight pink tentacles, which somewhat resemble flower petals. These tentacles are used to capture prey, which is then melted with a strong acid secreted by the tentacles. Its long, flexible neck has yellow bands in the center, and it can be extended to assist in capturing prey. Its body is short and squat with four stubby growths and a yellow, oval, target-like pattern on the chest. In order to prevent being washed away by ocean tides, the body of this Pokmon is heavy. In ancient times it
          <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_by_habitat#Sea_Pok.C3.A9mon" title="List of Pokmon by habitat">
           built its nest in the shallows of warm seas.
          </a>
          When the tide went out, it was seen on beaches.
         </p>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_anime">
           In the anime
          </span>
         </h2>
         <div class="thumb tleft">
          <div class="thumbinner" style="width:212px;">
           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wales_Island_Cradily.png">
            <img alt="" class="thumbimage" height="158" src="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/7/7e/Wales_Island_Cradily.png/210px-Wales_Island_Cradily.png" srcset="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/7/7e/Wales_Island_Cradily.png/315px-Wales_Island_Cradily.png 1.5x, http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/7/7e/Wales_Island_Cradily.png/420px-Wales_Island_Cradily.png 2x" width="210"/>
           </a>

         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Major_appearances">
           Major appearances
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          Cradily was first seen in
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/AG102" title="AG102">
            Where's Armaldo?
           </a>
          </i>
          on
          <a href="/wiki/Wales_Island" title="Wales Island">
           Wales Island
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Cradily also made an appearance in
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/DP108" title="DP108">
            Dealing With Defensive Types!
           </a>
          </i>
          with an
          <a href="/wiki/Armaldo_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Armaldo (Pokmon)">
           Armaldo
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Minor_appearances">
           Minor appearances
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          One made another cameo in
          <i>
           <a href="/wiki/M08" title="M08">
            Lucario and the Mystery of Mew
           </a>
          </i>
          living in the
          <a href="/wiki/Tree_of_Beginning" title="Tree of Beginning">
           Tree of Beginning
          </a>
          . Also, one appeared in the opening of the movie.
          <br clear="all"/>
         </p>

         <div class="thumb tright">
          <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">

         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_Pok.C3.A9mon_Adventures_manga">
           In the Pokmon Adventures manga
          </span>
         </h3>
         <p>
          In
          <a href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Adventures" title="Pokmon Adventures">
           Pokmon Adventures
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Roxanne" title="Roxanne">
           Roxanne
          </a>
          owns a Cradily, with which she battled
          <a href="/wiki/Magma_Admin_Courtney" title="Magma Admin Courtney">
           Courtney
          </a>
          and almost won until the
          <a href="/wiki/Magma_Admin_(Trainer_class)" title="Magma Admin (Trainer class)">
           Magma Admin
          </a>
          took three men hostage.
         </p>
         <p>
          A Cradily helped
          <a href="/wiki/Emerald_(Adventures)" title="Emerald (Adventures)">
           Emerald
          </a>
          when he was younger.
         </p>
         <p>
          Cradily is also used by the
          <a href="/wiki/Advanced_level_Grunt" title="Advanced level Grunt">
           Advanced level Grunt
          </a>
          of
          <a href="/wiki/Team_Galactic" title="Team Galactic">
           Team Galactic
          </a>
          . It was used in an attempt to stop
          <a href="/wiki/Diamond_(Adventures)" title="Diamond (Adventures)">
           Diamond
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="/wiki/Pearl_(Adventures)" title="Pearl (Adventures)">
           Pearl
          </a>
          , and
          <a href="/wiki/Platinum_(Adventures)" title="Platinum (Adventures)">
           Platinum
          </a>
          from releasing the
          <a href="/wiki/Lake_guardians" title="Lake guardians">
           lake guardians
          </a>
          from captivity.
         </p>

                <tr>
                 <th class="roundy" style="width: 80px; max-width: 80px; background:#A00000; border: 2px solid #A00000; line-height:12pt;">
                  <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Ruby" title="Pokmon Ruby">

                   </span>
                  </a>
                 </th>
                 <td class="roundy" style="vertical-align: middle; border: 1px solid #9DC1B7; padding-left:3px;">
                  Cradily roams around the ocean floor in search of food. This Pokmon freely extends its tree trunk-like neck and
                  <a href="/wiki/Constrict_(move)" title="Constrict (move)">
                   captures
                  </a>
                  unwary prey using its eight tentacles.

          <tr>
           <td class="roundybottom" colspan="7" style="background:#A7DB8D; font-size: 90%; line-height:10px;">
            <ul>
             <li>
              A level of "Start" indicates a move that will be known by a Cradily obtained at level 1 in Generation VI
             </li>
             <li>
              <b>
               Bold
              </b>
              indicates a move that gets
              <a href="/wiki/Same-type_attack_bonus" title="Same-type attack bonus">
               <span style="color:#000;">
                STAB
               </span>
              </a>
              when used by Cradily
             </li>
             <li>
              <i>
               Italic
              </i>
              indicates a move that gets STAB only when used by an evolution  of Cradily
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on the generation numbers at the top to see level-up moves from other generations
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>

          <tr>
           <td class="roundybottom" style="background:#A7DB8D; font-size: 90%; line-height:10px;">
            <ul>
             <li>
              Moves marked with an asterisk (*) must be
              <a href="/wiki/Chain_breeding" title="Chain breeding">
               <span style="color:#000;">
                chain bred
               </span>
              </a>
              onto Cradily in Generation VI
             </li>
             <li>
              Moves marked with a double dagger () can only be bred from a Pokmon who learned the move in an earlier generation.
             </li>
             <li>
              Moves marked with a superscript game abbreviation can only be bred onto Cradily in that game.
             </li>
             <li>
              <b>
               Bold
              </b>
              indicates a move that gets
              <a href="/wiki/Same-type_attack_bonus" title="Same-type attack bonus">
               <span style="color:#000;">
                STAB
               </span>
              </a>
              when used by Cradily
             </li>
             <li>
              <i>
               Italic
              </i>
              indicates a move that gets STAB only when used by an evolution  of Cradily
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on the generation numbers at the top to see Egg moves from other generations
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>

             </li>
             <li>
              <i>
               Italic
              </i>
              indicates a move that gets STAB only when used by an evolution  of Cradily
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on the generation numbers at the top to see moves from other generations
             </li>
            </ul>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>

         <br style="clear:both;"/>
         <h2>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">
           Trivia
          </span>
         </h2>
         <ul>
          <li>
           Cradily consists of the two types with most weaknesses,
           <a href="/wiki/Grass_(type)" title="Grass (type)">
            Grass
           </a>
           and
           <a href="/wiki/Rock_(type)" title="Rock (type)">
            Rock
           </a>
           , but it has only four weaknesses.
          </li>
          <li>
           Cradily is the only Pokmon with Pokathlon stats where each one is a different level.
          </li>
          <li>
           No other Pokmon has the same
           <a href="/wiki/Type" title="Type">
            type
           </a>
           <a href="/wiki/List_of_Pok%C3%A9mon_with_unique_type_combinations" title="List of Pokmon with unique type combinations">
            combination
           </a>
           as Cradily and its
           <a href="/wiki/Lileep_(Pok%C3%A9mon)" title="Lileep (Pokmon)">
            pre-evolution
           </a>
           .
          </li>
          <li>
           Cradily and its pre-evolution are the only Grass-type Pokmon that belong in the
           <a href="/wiki/Water_3_(Egg_Group)" title="Water 3 (Egg Group)">
            Water 3 Egg Group
           </a>
           .
          </li>
         </ul>
         <h3>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Origin">
           Origin
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="noprint" style="border-radius: 10px; -moz-border-radius: 10px; -webkit-border-radius: 10px; -khtml-border-radius: 10px; -icab-border-radius: 10px; -o-border-radius: 10px; clear: right; border: solid #88a 1px; margin: 0.25em 0 1em 1em; font-size: 90%; background: #f8f8ff; width: 250px; padding: 4px; spacing: 0px; text-align: left; float: right;">
          <div style="float: left;">
           <div class="floatnone">
            <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Bulbanews_logo.png" title="Bulbanews">
             <img alt="Bulbanews" height="57" src="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/9/96/Bulbanews_logo.png/50px-Bulbanews_logo.png" srcset="http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/9/96/Bulbanews_logo.png/75px-Bulbanews_logo.png 1.5x, http://cdn.bulbagarden.net/upload/thumb/9/96/Bulbanews_logo.png/100px-Bulbanews_logo.png 2x" width="50"/>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div style="margin-left: 60px;">
           <a class="extiw" href="http://bulbanews.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Front_page" title="n:Front page">
            <span style="color:#000;">
             Bulbanews
            </span>
           </a>
           has an article related to this subject:
           <div style="margin-left: 10px;">
            <i>
             <b>
              <a class="extiw" href="http://bulbanews.bulbagarden.net/wiki/On_the_Origin_of_Species:_Lileep_and_Cradily" title="n:On the Origin of Species: Lileep and Cradily">
               On the Origin of Species: Lileep and Cradily
              </a>
             </b>
            </i>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          It may be based on
          <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/crinoid" title="wp:crinoid">
           crinoids
          </a>
          , or
          <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sea_lily" title="wp:sea lily">
           sea lilies
          </a>
          , marine animals related to
          <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/seastar" title="wp:seastar">
           seastars
          </a>
          which were once believed to be extinct, or
          <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sea_anemone" title="wp:sea anemone">
           sea anemones
          </a>
          . It also bears resemblance to the
          <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/predatory_tunicate" title="wp:predatory tunicate">
           predatory tunicate
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <h4>
          <span class="mw-headline" id="Name_origin">
           Name origin
          </span>
         </h4>
         <p>
          Cradily may be a combination of
          <i>
           cradle
          </i>
          and
          <i>
           <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/lily" title="wp:lily">
            lily
           </a>
          </i>
          . It may also be a combination of
          <i>
           crag
          </i>
          or
          <i>
           crazily
          </i>
          and
          <i>
           lily
          </i>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Yuradle may be a combination of 
          <i>
           yuri
          </i>
          (lily) and
          <i>
           cradle
          </i>
          .
         </p>
